		( function( f ) {
			if ( document.readyState === 'loading' ) {
				document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', f );
			} else {
				f();
			}
		} )( function() {
			var regex = /r=[a-zA-Z0-9\.]*/g;
			var match = window.location.href.match( regex );

			if ( match !== null && match.length === 1 ) {
				var modal = document.querySelector( '.mfp-hide' );

				if ( ! modal ) {
					return;
				}

				modal.classList.remove( 'mfp-hide' );

				/**
				 * Add x-button handler and move it into form
				 */
				var xButton = document.getElementById( 'contact-overlay-x-button-outer' );

				if (xButton) {
					xButton.addEventListener( 'click', function() {
						document.getElementById( 'contact-overlay' ).remove();
						this.remove();
					} );

					var gform = document.querySelector('.gform_wrapper > form');
					if (gform) {
						gform.insertBefore(xButton, gform.firstElementChild);
						xButton.style.marginRight = '-40px';
						xButton.style.marginTop = '-40px';
						xButton.style.cursor = 'pointer';
					}		
				}

				var confirmation = document.querySelector('.gform_confirmation_wrapper');
				if (confirmation) {
					var contactOverlay = document.getElementById('contact-overlay');
					if (contactOverlay) {
						contactOverlay.style.display = 'none';
					}
				}

			}
		} );
	</script>

<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-282677f603fb2794f622b215657b1333" style="color:#222222">We have proven experience in launching, optimizing, and scaling media brands.</p>



<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-926097a2cc4e268f4c9d89cff9a9b091" style="color:#222222">The Publisher Desk was founded by Christopher Ward and Jeff Misenti, industry experts with backgrounds at News Corp and other digital ventures. <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-4104c1b098038d22c33e3767bcb895e7" style="color:#222222">The Publisher Desk is here to help. Founded by industry veterans, our goal is to give independent publishers access to the same tech and monetization strategies that the big names enjoy.</p>

<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-0d9d69d9874e4bc61fef266895f1e154" style="color:#222222">Think of GAM 360 as GAM’s big brother – more features, more control, and it’s tailored for the bigger players.</p>
</details>



<details class="wp-block-details has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-f70cadbefedf884dae26e3d4436fe3b1 is-layout-flow wp-block-details-is-layout-flow" style="color:#141414"><summary><a>Why go with a managed service?</a></summary>
<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-47279b4c01210c4c72697eef9c6d2187" style="color:#222222">Imagine having an all-star team focused solely on your growth, freeing you to create great content. That’s us.</p>
</details>



<details class="wp-block-details has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-5c308eb494a246232f6633a91f9ac3b3 is-layout-flow wp-block-details-is-layout-flow" style="color:#141414"><summary><a>How does personalized service make a difference?</a></summary>
<p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-9555c47dad4561b253a0647f058e3065" style="color:#222222">Your brand is unique, right? We think your growth strategy should be too. That’s why we tailor our strategies to your specific needs.</p>
</details>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
